|  | in which price is not agreed.Procurement contract should be supported with approved quotation comparison form (QCF). |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

|  | Procurement contract should be signed 6-month at longest subsequent to CAPEX investment proposal approved. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  | Otherwise, the proposal is subject to re-approval in case of business requirement change. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

|  | If the amount is foreign currency in the A2, converting into RMB is on the basis of the central parity rate in PBOC ,and the date is last day of the previous month of application. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

| N4： | 账面价值≤5万元的固定资产以旧换新CAPEX项目，报备时须附详细换新方案，获批后无需另行申请报废审批。账面价值≥5万元的固定资产以旧换新CAPEX项目，仍需进行cpaex报废流程 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| N4： | For CAPEX projects involving the trade-in replacement of fixed assets with a book value ≤ RMB50,000, a detailed replacement plan must be attached during the reporting process. Upon approval, a separate disposal approval is not required. For CAPEX projects involving the trade-in replacement of fixed assets with a book value ≥ RMB50,000, the standard CAPEX disposal procedure must still be followed |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| N5： | 当预见OPEX将超出预算时，必须在执行相关预算前完成超预算审批，方可发起立项审批。 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  | a) 无需单独进行预算外立项审批的费用类型包括： |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  | 与产量成比例的水、电、燃气等费用及成品检验费、原料检验费； |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  | 单一费用科目虽在单月超预算但未超累计预算的情况； |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  | 月度常规维修费超预算30%以内； |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  | 已立项报备的差旅费、招待费、团建费等；摊销折旧及租赁费。 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  | 通过采购流程实施的OPEX项目。 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  | b) 需要单独进行预算外立项审批的费用类型包括： |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  | 除前述费用以外的费用，包括办公费及其他类费用，如除成品、原料检验以外的检验费、环境卫生费； |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  | 常规维修费超预算30%以上需要OPEX超预算立项，预算外专项维修任何金额需要OPEX超预算立项； |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  | 品保专题项目，如新品、代工产品、应对质量投诉检测及公司内部增加检测项目等，应做专项报备。 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| N5： | When OPEX is expected to exceed the budget, out-of-budget approval must be completed before executing the budget. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  | a) Expenses exempt from separate out-of-budget approval: |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  | Costs proportional to production volume (e.g., water, electricity, gas) and inspection fees for finished products/raw materials. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  | Individual cost categories exceeding monthly budgets but within cumulative annual budgets. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  | Routine maintenance expenses exceeding monthly budgets by ≤30%. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  | Pre-approval and documented travel, entertainment, team-building, and similar expenses. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  | Amortization, depreciation, and leasing fees. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  | OPEX projects executed through procurement processes. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

|  | All other expenses not covered in a), including administrative costs, non-production/material inspection fees, and environmental/sanitation fees. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

| N3： | 含公司名称的发票专用章、品保章、食堂章等部门章由保管部门对使用情况和日常管理进行规范 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

| N4： | 法人章用印审批流参照该业务类型的公章用印审批流制定，使用法定代表人印章需要每半年向法定代表人提供用印清单 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| N4： | Please follow corporate seal usage flow for that of legal representative. A list of legal representative seal usage should be reported to himself on half-yearly basis |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| N5： | 不走标准采购流程直接用印的合同，如供应商为新加入的，均需要通过采购进行供应商背景调查，并按照新供应商注册审批，确保没有利益冲突 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| N5： | Procurement is in charge of qualification on a new supplier to ensure no conflict of interests with the company where purchases not under standard procurement process ( e.g. unloading soybean from vessel in government appointed port) |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| N6： | 新销售合同-标准销售合同用印，应在完成2.2页新销售合同-标准销售合同成交信息确认审批后申请 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| N6： | The printing of the new sales Contract-Standard sales Contract shall be applied after the confirmation and approval of the transaction information of the 2.2 pages of the New Sales Contract-Standard sales Contract |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

| N7： | Agreement not under standard procurement process" denote procurement operations for "categories not subject to procurement processes," as defined in the "Standard Procurement Process. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| N8： | 非常规业务指非计划内发生的、突发的、涉及公司合规状态改变、可能带来法律或财务风险、或需要高层决策介入的政府沟通与处置事项。通常涉及调查、处罚、申诉、重大承诺或新的行政许可申请。 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| N8： | Non-routine matters refer to unplanned, emergent communications or handling activities with government agencies or public institutions that involve changes in the company's compliance status or may entail legal or financial risks. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  | Such matters typically include investigations, penalties, appeals, material commitments, or applications for new administrative permits, and often require high-level decision-making intervention. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| **ACH = Agri Commercial Head |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

## A2.8 Credit Risk

| Code | Item | Sub-item | Amount (RMB'000) | Initiator | Department Head | Department Head | Department Head | Appr_9 | Approval Method |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
|  |  | Procurement Director | Procurement Director | Procurement Director | Procurement Director | Procurement Director |  |  |  |
|  |  | Finance Deputy Director | Finance Deputy Director | Finance Deputy Director | Finance Deputy Director | Finance Deputy Director |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  | DS Credit Manager | DS Credit Manager | Head of Risk & Compliance |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  | China CFO | China CFO | China CFO |  |  |  |
| Purchase (Non-trading) | Tenor | X≤36 months | X≤  12 months | X≤  12 months | X≤ 12 months | Beyond credit limit / tenor authorized in left table |  |  |  |
| Purchase (Non-trading) | Limit | X ≤RMB 30K | RMB 30K <  X≤RMB 100K | RMB 30K  <  X≤ RMB 100K | RMB 100K<  X ≤USD 50K | Beyond credit limit / tenor authorized in left table |  |  |  |
| Purchase (Non-trading) | % of contract amount | Up to 100% | ≤ 50% | > 50% | Up to 100% | Beyond credit limit / tenor authorized in left table |  |  |  |
| N1：Tenor（期限）是指交易合同的定价日与执行日（即交割日）之间的最长时间跨度（通常以合同日作为定价日的参考日期）。 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| N1：Tenor refers to the maximum period between pricing date and execution (delivery) date |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| of a trading contract (contract date as reference date for pricing date). |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| N2：单笔五万元以下的京东自营店预付款，无需按上述要求审批。 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| N2：Advance payments for JD self-operated stores of less than RMB 50,000 per transaction are exempt from the aforementioned approval requirements |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
